# debug.getconstant - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#debuggetconstant)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Debug/getconstant.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Debug/getconstant.md "View source of this page")

`debug.getconstant`
===================

C closures are not supported

This function will throw an error if called on a C closure, such as [`print`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#print)
, since C closures have no accessible constants.

`debug.getconstant` returns the constant at the specified index from a Luau function. If no constant exists at that index, it returns `nil` instead.

This is useful when you want to inspect specific constant values (such as strings, numbers, or booleans) without dumping the entire list.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-0-1) function debug.getconstant(func: (...any) -> (...any) | number, index: number): number | string | boolean | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `func` | The Luau function (or stack level) whose constant to retrieve. |
| `index` | The position of the desired constant. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Getting a valid constant |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local function dummy_function()     local dummy_string = "foo bar"    string.split(dummy_string, " ") end local result = debug.getconstant(dummy_function, 2) print(result) -- Output: string` |

### Example 2

| Getting an out-of-range constant |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getconstant/#__codelineno-2-7) | `local function dummy_function()     local dummy_string = "foo bar"    string.split(dummy_string, " ") end local result = debug.getconstant(dummy_function, 3) print(result) -- Output: nil` |

### Example 3

| Calling on a C closure should error |     |
| --- | --- |

# debug.getproto - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#debuggetproto)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Debug/getproto.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Debug/getproto.md "View source of this page")

`debug.getproto`
================

C closures are not supported

This function will throw an error if called on a C closure, such as [`print`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#print)
, since C closures do not contain function prototypes.

Inactive protos

Protos retrieved without the `activated` should not be callable; this leads to vulnerabilities. The usage of inactive protos is to retrieve information off of them.

`debug.getproto` returns a specific function prototype from a Luau function by index. Optionally, it can search for **active functions** of the proto, if the `activated` parameter is set to `true`.

These are internal function definitions (e.g. nested functions) that exist as part of the compiled bytecode, even if they aren't assigned or called.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-0-1) function debug.getproto(func: (...any) -> (...any) | number, index: number, activated: boolean?): (...any) -> (...any) | { (...any) -> (...any) }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `func` | The Luau function (or stack level) to extract a proto from. |
| `index` | The index of the prototype to return. |
| `activated?` | If `true`, returns a table of currently active functions based on the proto. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Retrieving nested prototypes |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-1-11) | `local function dummy_function()     local function dummy_proto_1()        print("Hello")    end    local function dummy_proto_2()        print("Hello2")    end end debug.getproto(dummy_function, 1)() -- Uncallable debug.getproto(dummy_function, 2)() -- Uncallable` |

### Example 2

| Retrieving an active function from a proto |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getproto/#__codelineno-2-12) | `local function dummy_function()     local function dummy_proto()        return "hi"    end    return dummy_proto end local real_proto = dummy_function() local retrieved_proto = debug.getproto(dummy_function, 1, true)[1] print(real_proto == retrieved_proto) -- Output: true print(retrieved_proto()) -- Output: hi` |

Back to top

# debug.setconstant - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#debugsetconstant)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Debug/setconstant.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Debug/setconstant.md "View source of this page")

`debug.setconstant`
===================

C closures are not supported

This function will throw an error if called on a C closure, such as [`print`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#print)
, since C closures have no accessible constants.

Mutable globals

If `game`is a mutable global, the constant indexes will be different.

`debug.setconstant` modifies a constant at the specified index in a Luau function bytecode.

This can be used to change hardcoded behavior within functions without modifying their source code - although it requires knowing the correct constant index beforehand.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-0-1) function debug.setconstant(func: (...any) -> (...any) | number, index: number, value: number | string | boolean | nil): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `func` | The Luau function (or stack level) whose constant to modify. |
| `index` | The position of the constant to change. |
| `value` | The new constant value to set. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Overwriting a constant string in a function |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setconstant/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local function dummy_function()     print(game.Name) end debug.setconstant(dummy_function, 4, "Players") dummy_function() -- Output: Players` |

`debug.getupvalue`
==================

C closures are not supported

`debug.getupvalue` returns the upvalue at the specified index from a Luau function's closure. If the index is invalid or out of bounds, an error will occur.

# debug.setstack - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#debugsetstack)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Debug/setstack.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Debug/setstack.md "View source of this page")

`debug.setstack`
================

C closures are not supported

This function will throw an error if the stack level points to a C closure, such as `setstack(0, 1, 0)`.

`debug.setstack` replaces a value in a specified stack frame.

This allows for powerful manipulation of runtime variables or arguments, particularly useful in advanced debugging or dynamic patching scenarios.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-0-1) function debug.setstack(level: number, index: number, value: any): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `level` | The stack level to target. `1` refers to the current function. |
| `index` | The index/slot in the stack frame to replace. |
| `value` | The new value to assign at that stack slot. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Replacing the 'error' function on the stack with our own |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-1-5) | `error(debug.setstack(1, 1, function()     return function()        print("Replaced")    end end))() -- Output: Replaced` |

### Example 2

| Replacing a numeric local in a parent scope |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-8)<br>[9](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/setstack/#__codelineno-2-9) | `local outer_value = 10 local function inner_function()     outer_value += 9    debug.setstack(2, 1, 100) end inner_function() print(outer_value) -- Output: 100` |

C closures not supported

`debug.setupvalue` replaces an upvalue at the specified index in a Luau function, with a new value.

This allows for controlled modification of function state, often used in hooking or testing environments.

# debug.getupvalues - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#debuggetupvalues)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Debug/getupvalues.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Debug/getupvalues.md "View source of this page")

`debug.getupvalues`
===================

C closures are not supported

This function will throw an error if called on a C closure, such as [`print`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#print)
, for security reasons.

`debug.getupvalues` returns a list of upvalues captured by a Luau function. These are the external variables that a function closes over from its surrounding scope.

If the function has no upvalues, the result will be an empty table.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-0-1) function debug.getupvalues(func: (...any) -> (...any) | number): { any }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `func` | The Luau function (or stack level) to retrieve upvalues from. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Retrieving upvalues from a closure |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-14)<br>[15](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-1-15) | `local var1 = false local var2 = "Hi" local function dummy_function()     var1 = true    var2 ..= ", hello" end for index, value in pairs(debug.getupvalues(dummy_function)) do     print(index, value) end -- Output: -- 1 false -- 2 Hi` |

### Example 2

| Calling with a function that has no upvalues |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-2-5) | `local function dummy_function()     return 123 end print(next(debug.getupvalues(dummy_function))) -- Output: nil` |

### Example 3

| Calling on a C closure should error |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Debug/getupvalues/#__codelineno-3-1) | `print(debug.getupvalues(print)) -- Should error due to being a C closure` |

# Drawing class - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/#drawing-class)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Drawing/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Drawing/README.md "View source of this page")

Drawing class
=============

The `Drawing` class represents a renderable 2D object that appears on the user's screen. Every specific drawing type (e.g. `Circle`, `Text`, `Line`) inherits from this base and extends it with shape-specific properties.

Drawing objects are **_not_** instances - they are client-only graphical primitives that do not interact with the 3D world and must be managed manually.

* * *

Constructor
-----------

Creates a new render object of the specified type. These objects render directly onto the game window and do not exist in the [`DataModel`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/DataModel)
.

Inheritance

The returned object inherits from the base `Drawing` class, and will have specific properties based on its type.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/#__codelineno-0-1) function Drawing.new(type: string): Drawing`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `type` | The type of drawing to create. Must be one of: [`Line`, `Text`, `Image`, `Circle`, `Square`, `Quad`, or `Triangle`](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/#shape-specific-types)<br>. |

* * *

Shared properties
-----------------

Note about the behaviour of the `Transparency` property

Some implementations of the Drawing library by executors have mistakenly treated the `Transparency` property as **opacity** rather than actual **transparency**. This confusion originates from the original UNC documentation, which incorrectly defined _transparency_ as _"the opacity of the drawing"_ (quite literally wrong, the opposite!).

![Definition of the word "Transparency"](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/assets/transparency.png)

In sUNC, we follow the correct meaning of the word. `Transparency` represents true transparency, where `0` means fully opaque and `1` means fully **transparent** (see-through). This also aligns with how Roblox handles their transparency property on some instances (e.g. Part, Frame, etc).

All drawing object types inherit the following fields:

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Visible` | `boolean` | Whether the object is rendered. Defaults to `false`. |
| `ZIndex` | `number` | Render order; higher values appear on top. |
| `Transparency` | `number` | Translucency, where `1` is fully transparent and `0` is fully visible. |
| `Color` | `Color3` | The color of the drawing. |
| `__OBJECT_EXISTS` | `boolean` | Whether the drawing object exists. |

* * *

Methods
-------

| Method Signature | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Destroy()` | Permanently removes the drawing from view. |

* * *

Shape-specific types
--------------------

Each subtype of `Drawing` exposes unique fields that define their visual representation. Below are the supported types:

### Line

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `From` | `Vector2` | Start position of the line. |
| `To` | `Vector2` | End position of the line. |
| `Thickness` | `number` | Width of the line. |

### Text

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Text` | `string` | The text content to render. |
| `TextBounds` | `Vector2` 🔒 | Computed text size (read-only). |
| `Font` | `Drawing.Font` | Font to use. |
| `Size` | `number` | Size of the text. |
| `Position` | `Vector2` | Top-left corner of the text. |
| `Center` | `boolean` | Horizontally center the text. |
| `Outline` | `boolean` | Whether to draw an outline. |
| `OutlineColor` | `Color3` | Outline color. |

### Image

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Data` | `string` | Raw image byte string (e.g. from [`readfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/)<br>). |
| `Size` | `Vector2` | Size of the rendered image. |
| `Position` | `Vector2` | Top-left corner of the image. |
| `Rounding` | `number` | Amount of corner rounding (optional aesthetic). |

### Circle

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `NumSides` | `number` | Number of sides used to approximate the circle. |
| `Radius` | `number` | Radius of the circle. |
| `Position` | `Vector2` | Center point of the circle. |
| `Thickness` | `number` | Outline thickness (if not filled). |
| `Filled` | `boolean` | Whether the circle is filled. |

### Square

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Size` | `Vector2` | Size of the rectangle. |
| `Position` | `Vector2` | Top-left corner. |
| `Thickness` | `number` | Outline thickness (if not filled). |
| `Filled` | `boolean` | Whether the square is filled. |

### Quad

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `PointA` | `Vector2` | First point. |
| `PointB` | `Vector2` | Second point. |
| `PointC` | `Vector2` | Third point. |
| `PointD` | `Vector2` | Fourth point. |
| `Thickness` | `number` | Outline thickness (if not filled). |
| `Filled` | `boolean` | Whether the quad is filled. |

### Triangle

| Property | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `PointA` | `Vector2` | First point. |
| `PointB` | `Vector2` | Second point. |
| `PointC` | `Vector2` | Third point. |
| `Thickness` | `number` | Outline thickness (if not filled). |
| `Filled` | `boolean` | Whether the triangle is filled. |

Examples
--------

### Using the `Destroy` method

| Creating a circle and destroying the drawing object |     |
| --- | --- |

# Encoding - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/#encoding)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Encoding/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Encoding/README.md "View source of this page")

Encoding
========

The **Encoding** library provides functions for common binary transformation operations such as Base64 and LZ4 - the **encoding**, **decoding**, **compression**, and **decompression** of data.

This library replaces the old `crypt` library, which has now been fully deprecated.

* * *

Where is the `crypt` library?
-----------------------------

sUNC has not tested the `crypt` library in a very long time now. In fact, the last remaining functions that we _did_ test, Base64, did not deserve to be in the `crypt` category.

This is due to multiple reasons, but mainly because having cryptography functions available in an executor's environment is not safe because other scripts can easily redefine them to hijack potentially sensitive information. For anyone who requires cryptography, we advise you to just inline/"bring your own" cryptography functions in your code and use it from there.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Encoding library, you can:

*   **Encode and decode** binary or text data into Base64 using [`base64encode`](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/base64encode/)
     and [`base64decode`](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/base64decode/)
    
*   **Compress and decompress** data efficiently using the LZ4 algorithm with [`lz4compress`](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4compress/)
     and [`lz4decompress`](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/)
    

* * *

What are Base64 and LZ4?
------------------------

**Base64** is a [binary-to-text encoding scheme](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Base64)
 that represents binary data using ASCII characters, making it suitable for embedding in text-based formats such as JSON or XML.

**LZ4** is a [lossless data compression algorithm](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LZ4_(compression_algorithm))
 known for its high speed and low latency.

* * *

What can't you do?
------------------

*   These functions are designed for data transformation only and are **not** encryption methods designed to replace any previous `crypt` functions. They do not provide confidentiality or security.

Back to top

---

# isrenderobj - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#isrenderobj)

`isrenderobj`
=============

`isrenderobj` checks whether a given value is a valid [`Drawing`](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/)
 object.

This is useful for validation in functions or modules that work with custom render systems.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-0-1) function isrenderobj(object: any): boolean`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object` | The value to check for Drawing validity. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Checking if an object is a render object |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/isrenderobj/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local square = Drawing.new("Square") print(isrenderobj(square))       -- Output: true print(isrenderobj(workspace))    -- Output: false print(isrenderobj("not a draw")) -- Output: false` |

# getrenderproperty - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#getrenderproperty)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Drawing/getrenderproperty.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Drawing/getrenderproperty.md "View source of this page")

`getrenderproperty`
===================

`getrenderproperty` retrieves the value of a property from a [`Drawing`](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/)
 object. This behaves identically to using `object[property]`, but is useful when working with dynamic property names or for reflection-like access.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-0-1) function getrenderproperty(drawing: Drawing, property: string): any`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `drawing` | A valid [`Drawing`](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/)<br> object. |
| `property` | The name of the property to retrieve. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Reading drawing properties |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Drawing/getrenderproperty/#__codelineno-1-6) | `local circle = Drawing.new("Circle") circle.Radius = 50 circle.Visible = true print(getrenderproperty(circle, "Radius"))    -- Output: 50 print(getrenderproperty(circle, "Visible"))   -- Output: true` |

Back to top

| `value` | The value to assign to the specified property. |

* * *

Example

| Setting drawing properties |     |
| --- | --- |

# Environment - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/#environment)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/README.md "View source of this page")

Environment
===========

The **Environment** library allows access and inspection to our and Roblox's environment.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Environment library, you can:

*   **Access and modify executor globals** using [`getgenv`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/)
    
*   **Modify the game global environment** using [`getrenv`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/)
    
*   **View collectable and living values** using [`getgc`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/)
    
*   **Filter** garbage-collected values with fine-tuned criteria using [`filtergc`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/)
    

Back to top

---

# lz4decompress - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/#lz4decompress)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Encoding/lz4decompress.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Encoding/lz4decompress.md "View source of this page")

`lz4decompress`
===============

`lz4decompress` decompresses a string that was encoded using the [LZ4](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LZ4_(compression_algorithm))
 compression algorithm back to regular data.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/#__codelineno-0-1) function lz4decompress(data: string): string`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `data` | The string to decompress. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Decompressing an LZ4 encoded string back to regular data |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Encoding/lz4decompress/#__codelineno-1-3) | `local text = "Hello, world! Hello, world!" local compressed = lz4compress(text) print(lz4decompress(compressed, #text)) -- "Hello, world! Hello, world!"` |

# getrenv - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#getrenv)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/getrenv.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/getrenv.md "View source of this page")

`getrenv`
=========

Adding `_G` and `shared`

Make sure to properly implement `_G` and `shared` into the Roblox environment, as poor implementations will result in detection vectors!

`getrenv` returns the **Roblox global environment**, which is used by the entire game. Changes to this environment will affect your executor environment as well.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-0-1) function getrenv(): { any }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Overriding Roblox environment functions |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getrenv/#__codelineno-1-5) | `getrenv().warn = "Hello!" print(type(warn)) -- Output: string getrenv().game = nil print(game) -- Output: nil` |

Back to top

---

# getgenv - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#getgenv)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/getgenv.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/getgenv.md "View source of this page")

`getgenv`
=========

Pollution of getgenv results

Modifications to a thread's global environment should not affect the results returned by `getgenv`.

`getgenv` returns the **executor's global environment table**, which is shared across all executor-made threads.

This environment is writable and persistent during the session, making it useful for sharing state or functions across different scripts.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-0-1) function getgenv(): { any }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| getgenv should not be affected by the global table/getfenv |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgenv/#__codelineno-1-8) | `getgenv().dummy_val = "value" getfenv().dummy_val_2 = 1 print(dummy_val, getgenv().dummy_val_2) -- Output: value, 1 getgenv().dummy_val = "value2" dummy_val = nil print(dummy_val) -- Output: value2` |

Back to top

---

# getgc - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#getgc)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/getgc.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/getgc.md "View source of this page")

`getgc`
=======

`getgc` returns a list of **non-dead garbage-collectable values**. These include functions, userdatas, and optionally tables.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-1) export type AnyFunction = (...any) -> (...any) [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-2) export type AnyTable = { [any]: any } [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-3)[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-4) export type userdata = typeof(newproxy()) -- (1) [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-5)[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-6) declare getgc:     [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-7)     ((includeTables: true) -> { { AnyTable } | AnyFunction | userdata }) &    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-0-8)     ((includeTables: false?) -> { AnyFunction })`

1.  Note that `userdata` is not an official Luau type, but we define it here for clarity - because `getgc` can return them as part of its results.

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `includeTables?` | If `true`, also includes tables in the returned list. Defaults to `false`. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Function-only GC scan |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-1-11) | ``local dummy_table = {} local function dummy_function() end task.wait(0.05) -- Step a bit for _, value in pairs(getgc()) do     if value == dummy_function then        print(`Found function: {dummy_function}`)    elseif value == dummy_table then        print(`Found table?: {dummy_table}`) -- This shouldn't print    end end`` |

### Example 2

| Full GC scan including tables |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/#__codelineno-2-11) | ``local dummy_table = {} local function dummy_function() end task.wait(0.05) -- Step a bit for _, value in pairs(getgc(true)) do     if value == dummy_function then        print(`Found function: {dummy_function}`) -- Should print    elseif value == dummy_table then        print(`Found table: {dummy_table}`) -- Should also print    end end`` |

Back to top

# getreg - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#getreg)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/getreg.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/getreg.md "View source of this page")

`getreg`
========

`getreg` returns the **Luau registry table**. The registry is a special table which is used internally to store references like threads, functions, and data shared between C and Luau (userdata).

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-0-1) function getreg(): { [any]: any }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Closing a thread via getreg |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-14)<br>[15](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-15)<br>[16](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getreg/#__codelineno-1-16) | ``local loop_thread = task.spawn(function()     while task.wait(1) do        print("I am still running...")    end end) task.wait(0.2) -- Let the loop run for a bit for _, value in pairs(getreg()) do     if value ~= loop_thread then continue end     print(`Found loop thread: {loop_thread}`) -- Should print    coroutine.close(loop_thread) -- Should close the thread     break end`` |

# filtergc - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#filtergc)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/README.md "View source of this page")

`filtergc`
==========

`filtergc` allows you to retrieve specific garbage-collected values from Luau's memory, using fine-tuned filters.

This function is most often used to find game-defined functions or internal tables by matching constants, keys, metatables, and more. It behaves similarly to [`getgc`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/getgc/)
, but offers simplicity, efficiency, and more control over what gets returned.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-1) export type AnyFunction = (...any) -> (...any) [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-2) export type AnyTable = { [any]: any } [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-3)[](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-4) declare filtergc:      [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-5)     (( filterType: "function", filterOptions: FunctionFilterOptions, returnOne: true) -> AnyFunction? ) &    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-6)     ((( filterType: "function", filterOptions: FunctionFilterOptions, returnOne: false?) -> ( AnyFunction | { AnyFunction } ) )) &    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-7)     (( filterType: "table", filterOptions: TableFilterOptions, returnOne: true) -> { AnyTable? } ) &    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#__codelineno-0-8)     (( filterType: "table", filterOptions: TableFilterOptions, returnOne: false? ) -> { AnyTable })`

* * *

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `filterType` | The type of value to search for. |
| `filterOptions` | A set of rules used to match functions or tables. [See below.](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/#filter-option-types) |
| `returnOne?` | If `true`, returns the first match, instead of a table of matches. |

* * *

Filter option types
-------------------

Each filter type has its own valid fields:

*   See [Function Filters](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/)
     for matching functions by name, constants, upvalues, and more.
*   See [Table Filters](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/)
     for matching tables by keys, values, metatables, and more.

* * *

Notes
-----

*   Garbage-collected values must still be referenced by a live thread to be found.
*   Some filters (like `Constants` or `Hash`) do not apply to C functions.

Back to top

---

# Filesystem - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/#filesystem)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/README.md "View source of this page")

Filesystem
==========

The **Filesystem** library provides access to an executor's virtual file system. It enables reading, writing, creating, and deleting files and folders, as well as utility functions for interacting with content assets.

This library is especially useful when storing persistent data, managing resources across sessions, or loading runtime content dynamically.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Filesystem library, you can:

*   **Write** data to a file using [`writefile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/writefile/)
    
*   **Read** file contents with [`readfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/)
    
*   **Append** content using [`appendfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/)
    
*   **List** files and folders via [`listfiles`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/)
    
*   **Delete** files with [`delfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/delfile/)
     and folders using [`delfolder`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/delfolder/)
    
*   **Check** if a path is a file or folder using [`isfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfile/)
     or [`isfolder`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/)
    
*   **Create** folders with [`makefolder`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/makefolder/)
    
*   **Dynamically load** code from a file via [`loadfile`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/)
    
*   **Use** local assets in Roblox via [`getcustomasset`](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/)
    , as if it were an uploaded asset

* * *

What can't you do?
------------------

*   You cannot access files outside the executor's workspace/sandboxed storage
*   You cannot use file IO to interact with the real disk (e.g. `C:/` (Windows), `/Library` (macOS), etc.)
*   You cannot escape the executor's `workspace` folder at all.

Back to top

---

# appendfile - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/#appendfile)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/appendfile.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/appendfile.md "View source of this page")

`appendfile`
============

`appendfile` appends string content to the end of a file at the specified path. If the file does not exist, it will be created.

This is useful for logging, accumulating data over time, or extending file contents without overwriting them.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/#__codelineno-0-1) function appendfile(path: string, contents: string): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The file path to append to. |
| `contents` | The string content to add to the file. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Appending to a file |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/appendfile/#__codelineno-1-3) | `writefile("file4.txt", "print(") appendfile("file4.txt", "'Hello')") print(readfile("file4.txt")) -- Output: print('Hello')` |

# getcustomasset - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#getcustomasset)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/getcustomasset.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/getcustomasset.md "View source of this page")

`getcustomasset`
================

`getcustomasset` returns a content ID (e.g. `rbxasset://`) that can be used in Roblox APIs for loading audio, meshes, UI images, and other asset types.

Internally, the file at the given path is copied to the game's content directory and then exposed with a usable asset URL.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-0-1) function getcustomasset(path: string): string`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The file path to convert into an asset ID. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Using getcustomasset to load and play a sound in-game |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/getcustomasset/#__codelineno-1-10) | `local encoded = game:HttpGet("https://gitlab.com/sens3/nebunu/-/raw/main/encodedBytecode.txt") writefile("ExampleSound.mp3", base64decode(encoded)) local asset_id = getcustomasset("ExampleSound.mp3") local sound = Instance.new("Sound") sound.Parent = workspace sound.SoundId = asset_id sound.Volume = 0.35 sound:Play()` |

# Table filter options - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#table-filter-options)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions.md "View source of this page")

Table filter options
====================

Table filters define what types of Luau tables should be returned when using [`filtergc`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/)
 with `"table"` as the filter type.

Each key in the filter table specifies a condition the table must meet in order to be returned. You can use one or multiple fields together to narrow your results.

* * *

Available Options
-----------------

| Key | Type | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `Keys` | `{ any }?` | If provided, also includes tables that contain **all** the specified keys. | `nil` |
| `Values` | `{ any }?` | If provided, only includes tables that contain **all** the specified values. | `nil` |
| `KeyValuePairs` | `{ [any]: any }?` | If provided, only includes tables that contain **all** key-value pairs in this table. | `nil` |
| `Metatable` | `table?` | If provided, only includes tables whose metatable matches the given one. | `nil` |

* * *

Notes
-----

*   These filters work based on narrowing - the more information you provide in the filters, the more accurate the result.
*   If `Metatable` is used, a raw metatable comparison is performed.

Examples
--------

False negatives may occur

Executing these examples multiple times in a short period of time may result in false negatives.

### Matching by `Keys`

| Matching a table by key |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-7) | `local dummy_table = { ["dummy_key"] = "" } local retrieved = filtergc("table", {     Keys = { "dummy_key" }, }, true) print(retrieved == dummy_table) -- Output: true` |

### Matching by `KeyValuePairs`

| Matching a table by key-value pairs |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local dummy_table = { ["dummy_key"] = "dummy_value" } local retrieved = filtergc("table", {     KeyValuePairs = { ["dummy_key"] = "dummy_value" }, }, true) print(retrieved == dummy_table) -- Output: true` |

### Matching by `Metatable`

| Matching a table by metatable |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-7) | `local dummy_table = setmetatable({}, { __index = getgenv() }) local retrieved = filtergc("table", {      Metatable = getmetatable(dummy_table)  }, true) print(retrieved == dummy_table) -- Output: true` |

### Type signature for `TableFilterOptions`

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/TableFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-6) | `type TableFilterOptions = {     Keys: { [any]: any }?,    Values: { [any]: any }?,    KeyValuePairs: { [any]: any }?,    Metatable: { [any]: any }?, }` |

Back to top

---

# isfolder - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#isfolder)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/isfolder.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/isfolder.md "View source of this page")

`isfolder`
==========

`isfolder` checks whether a given path exists and refers to a folder.

This is useful when verifying that a directory exists before writing files into it or listing its contents.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#__codelineno-0-1) function isfolder(path: string): boolean`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The path to check. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Checking folder existence |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/isfolder/#__codelineno-1-4) | `writefile("file7.txt", "") makefolder("folder2") print(isfolder("file7.txt")) -- Output: false print(isfolder("folder2"))   -- Output: true` |

# Function filter options - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#function-filter-options)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions.md "View source of this page")

Function filter options
=======================

Function filters let you refine what types of Luau functions should be returned when using [`filtergc`](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/)
 with `"function"` as the filter type.

Each key in the filter table specifies a criterion that must be matched by the function for it to be returned. You can use one or multiple fields together to narrow your results.

* * *

Available options
-----------------

| Key | Type | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `Name` | `string?` | If provided, filters out functions which don't match this name. | `nil` |
| `IgnoreExecutor` | `boolean?` | If `true`, filters out functions that were created inside the executor. | `true` |
| `Hash` | `string?` | Filters by the hash of the function. See [`getfunctionhash`](https://docs.sunc.su/Closures/getfunctionhash/)<br>. | `nil` |
| `Constants` | `{ any }?` | Also includes functions that contain the matching constants in the provided list. | `nil` |
| `Upvalues` | `{ any }?` | Also includes functions that contain the matching upvalues in the provided list. | `nil` |

* * *

Notes
-----

*   These filters work based on narrowing - the more information you provide in the filters, the more accurate the final result.
*   If `IgnoreExecutor` is not explicitly set to `false`, executor-created functions are skipped by default.
*   Filters like `Constants`, `Upvalues`, and `Hash` do not apply to C closures.

* * *

Examples
--------

False negatives may occur

Executing these examples multiple times in a short period of time may result in false negatives.

### Using `Name` (returns a `table` by default)

| Matching a function by name |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-8)<br>[9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-0-9) | `local function dummy_function() end local retrieved = filtergc("function", {     Name = "dummy_function",    IgnoreExecutor = false }) print(typeof(retrieved)) -- Output: table print(retrieved[1] == dummy_function) -- Output: true` |

* * *

### Using `Name` with `returnOne = true`

| Single match using returnOne |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-1-10) | `local function dummy_function()  end local retrieved = filtergc("function", {     Name = "dummy_function",    IgnoreExecutor = false }, true) print(typeof(retrieved)) -- Output: function print(retrieved == dummy_function) -- Output: true` |

* * *

### Using `Hash`

| Matching a function by hash |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-2-13) | `local function dummy_function()     return "Hello" end local dummy_function_hash = getfunctionhash(dummy_function) local retrieved = filtergc("function", {     Hash = dummy_function_hash,    IgnoreExecutor = false }, true) print(getfunctionhash(retrieved) == dummy_function_hash) -- Output: true print(retrieved == dummy_function) -- Output: true` |

### Matching by `Constants` and `Upvalues`

| Matching by function constants and upvalues |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-3-14) | `local upvalue = 5 local function dummy_function()     upvalue += 1    print(game.Players.LocalPlayer) end local retrieved = filtergc("function", {     Constants = { "print", "game", "Players", "LocalPlayer", 1 },    Upvalues = { 5 },    IgnoreExecutor = false }, true) print(retrieved == dummy_function) -- Output: true` |

### Type signature for `FunctionFilterOptions`

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Environment/filtergc/FunctionFilterOptions/#__codelineno-4-7) | `type FunctionFilterOptions = {     Name: string?,    IgnoreExecutor: boolean?,    Hash: string?,    Constants: { string }?,    Upvalues: { any }? }` |

# listfiles - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#listfiles)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/listfiles.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/listfiles.md "View source of this page")

`listfiles`
===========

Relative Paths

Please note that paths returned by `listfiles` are relative to the workspace folder of the executor.

`listfiles` returns an array of strings representing all files and folders within the specified directory.

This can be used to dynamically check which files exist in a folder, etc.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-0-1) function listfiles(path: string): { string }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The path to the directory to scan. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Listing files in the root directory |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/listfiles/#__codelineno-1-12) | ``writefile("file1.txt", "") writefile("file2.lua", "") task.wait() for _, file in listfiles("") do     if file == "file1.txt" then        print(`Found: {file}`) -- Output: Found: file1.txt    end    if file == "file2.lua" then        print(`Found: {file}`) -- Output: Found: file2.lua    end end`` |

# loadfile - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#loadfile)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/loadfile.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/loadfile.md "View source of this page")

`loadfile`
==========

`loadfile` compiles the Luau source code from a file and returns the resulting function (chunk). This chunk runs in the global environment.

If the file contains syntax errors, an error is thrown - just like [`loadstring`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#loadstring)
. The error will appear in the console.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-0-1) function loadfile<A...>(path: string): ((A...) -> any | nil, string?)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The path to the file to be loaded. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Loading and executing a valid file |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-1-3) | `writefile("file6.lua", "return 10 + ...") local chunk = loadfile("file6.lua") print(chunk(1)) -- Output: 11` |

### Example 2

| Triggering a syntax error |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/loadfile/#__codelineno-2-2) | `writefile("file6.lua", "retrn 10 + ...") loadfile("file6.lua") -- This will throw an error in the console` |

Back to top

---

# Instances - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/#instances)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/README.md "View source of this page")

Instances
=========

The **Instances** library provides direct access to and manipulation of [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 objects in the game world. It includes tools for listing, referencing, and firing Roblox-native interactions.

These functions are especially useful for inspecting hidden instances, working with UI safely, or simulating player interactions with in-game objects.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Instances library, you can:

*   **List all objects** tracked by the client using [`getinstances`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/)
    
*   **List nil-parented objects** using [`getnilinstances`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/)
    
*   **Compare two objects** using [`compareinstances`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/)
    
*   **Safely clone instance references** using [`cloneref`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/)
    
*   **Access hidden UI containers** using [`gethui`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/gethui/)
    
*   **Inspect function-based properties** with [`getcallbackvalue`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/)
    
*   **Simulate interactions** using [`fireclickdetector`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/)
    , [`fireproximityprompt`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/)
    , and [`firetouchinterest`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/)
    

Back to top

---

# readfile - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/#readfile)

`readfile`
==========

`readfile` retrieves the contents of a file at the specified path and returns it as a string.

If the file does not exist or cannot be accessed, the function will **error**.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/#__codelineno-0-1) function readfile(path: string): string`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The file path to read from. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Reading a file |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/readfile/#__codelineno-1-2) | `writefile("file0.txt", "Hello") print(readfile("file0.txt")) -- Output: Hello` |

# writefile - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/writefile/#writefile)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Filesystem/writefile.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Filesystem/writefile.md "View source of this page")

`writefile`
===========

`writefile` writes data to a file at the specified path. If the file already exists, its contents will be overwritten.

This is one of the primary ways to persist string data within the executor's file sandbox.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/writefile/#__codelineno-0-1) function writefile(path: string, data: string): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `path` | The file path to write to. |
| `data` | The string data to write into the file. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Basic file writing example |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/writefile/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Filesystem/writefile/#__codelineno-1-2) | `writefile("file.txt", "Hello world") print(readfile("file.txt")) -- Output: Hello world` |

Back to top

# compareinstances - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#compareinstances)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/compareinstances.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/compareinstances.md "View source of this page")

`compareinstances`
==================

`compareinstances` checks if two [`Instances`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 are equal.

This is primarily used for instances which have been [`cloneref`](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/)
'd, where the normal equality check with `==` fails.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#__codelineno-0-1) function compareinstances(object1: Instance, object2: Instance): boolean`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object1` | This first [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> to compare. |
| `object2` | The second [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> to compare against. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Comparing instances |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/compareinstances/#__codelineno-1-4) | `print(compareinstances(game, game))              -- true print(compareinstances(game, workspace))         -- false print(compareinstances(game, cloneref(game)))    -- true print(game == cloneref(game))                    -- false` |

Back to top

---

# getcallbackvalue - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#getcallbackvalue)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/getcallbackvalue.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/getcallbackvalue.md "View source of this page")

`getcallbackvalue`
==================

`getcallbackvalue` retrieves the **assigned callback property** on an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
, such as [`OnInvoke`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BindableFunction#OnInvoke)
.

Normally, these properties are **write-only**, meaning you can assign a function to them but cannot read them back. This function bypasses that limitation and exposes the function directly.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-0-1) function getcallbackvalue(object: Instance, property: string): any | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object` | The [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> that owns the callback property. |
| `property` | The name of the callback property to retrieve. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Retrieving a valid callback function, an unset property, and a missing property |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getcallbackvalue/#__codelineno-1-11) | `local dummy_bindable = Instance.new("BindableFunction") local dummy_remote_function = Instance.new("RemoteFunction") dummy_bindable.OnInvoke = function()     print("Hello from callback!") end local retrieved = getcallbackvalue(dummy_bindable, "OnInvoke") retrieved() -- Output: Hello from callback! print(getcallbackvalue(dummy_remote_function, "OnClientInvoke")) -- Output: nil` |

Back to top

---

# cloneref - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#cloneref)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/cloneref.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/cloneref.md "View source of this page")

`cloneref`
==========

Creates a safe reference to protected instances

`cloneref` returns a reference to an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
. This can help avoid weak table styled detections.

`cloneref` returns a **reference clone** of an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
. The returned object behaves identically to the original but is not strictly equal (`==`) to it.

This is commonly used to safely interact with services such as [`game.CoreGui`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Players#LocalPlayer)
, making weak-table style attacks fail.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-0-1) function cloneref<T>(object: T & Instance): T`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object` | The [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> to clone a safe reference from. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Cloning a safe reference to LocalPlayer |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/cloneref/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local players = game:GetService("Players") local original = players.LocalPlayer local clone = cloneref(original) print(original == clone) -- Output: false print(clone.Name)        -- Output: Player's name (same as original)` |

# fireproximityprompt - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#fireproximityprompt)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/fireproximityprompt.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/fireproximityprompt.md "View source of this page")

`fireproximityprompt`
=====================

Avoid implementing in Luau

This function should **not be implemented** in Luau. Doing so exposes you to easy detection vectors.

`fireproximityprompt` instantly triggers a [`ProximityPrompt`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ProximityPrompt)
, bypassing its [`HoldDuration`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ProximityPrompt#HoldDuration)
 and activation distance.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-0-1) function fireproximityprompt(prompt: ProximityPrompt): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `prompt` | The [`ProximityPrompt`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ProximityPrompt)<br> to trigger. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Triggering a ProximityPrompt manually |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-8)<br>[9](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireproximityprompt/#__codelineno-1-9) | `local part = Instance.new("Part", workspace) local prompt = Instance.new("ProximityPrompt", part) prompt.ActionText = "Click Me" prompt.Triggered:Connect(function(player)     print(player.Name .. " triggered the prompt") end) fireproximityprompt(prompt) -- Output: [YourName] triggered the prompt` |
