# fireclickdetector - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#fireclickdetector)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/fireclickdetector.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/fireclickdetector.md "View source of this page")

`fireclickdetector`
===================

Avoid implementing in Luau

This function should **not be implemented** in Luau. Doing so exposes you to easy detection vectors.

`fireclickdetector` triggers a [`ClickDetector`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ClickDetector)
 event. By default, it fires the [`MouseClick`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ClickDetector#MouseClick)
 event.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-0-1) function fireclickdetector(detector: ClickDetector, distance: number?, event: string?): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `detector` | The [`ClickDetector`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ClickDetector)<br> to trigger. |
| `distance?` | Distance from which the click is simulated. Defaults to infinite. |
| `event?` | The event to trigger. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Firing different ClickDetector events |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-14)<br>[15](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-15)<br>[16](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-16)<br>[17](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-17)<br>[18](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-18)<br>[19](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-19)<br>[20](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-20)<br>[21](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-21)<br>[22](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/fireclickdetector/#__codelineno-1-22) | ``local click_detector = Instance.new("ClickDetector") click_detector.MouseClick:Connect(function(player)     print(`{player.Name} Fired M1`) end) click_detector.RightMouseClick:Connect(function(player)     print(`{player.Name} Fired M2`) end) click_detector.MouseHoverEnter:Connect(function(player)     print(`{player.Name} Fired HoverEnter`) end) click_detector.MouseHoverLeave:Connect(function(player)     print(`{player} Fired HoverLeave`) end) fireclickdetector(click_detector, 0, "MouseClick") -- Output: Player Fired M1 fireclickdetector(click_detector, 0, "RightMouseClick") -- Output: Player Fired M2 fireclickdetector(click_detector, 0, "MouseHoverEnter") -- Output: Player Fired HoverEnter fireclickdetector(click_detector, 0, "MouseHoverLeave") -- Output: Player Fired HoverLeave`` |

# getinstances - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#getinstances)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/getinstances.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/getinstances.md "View source of this page")

`getinstances`
==============

Includes all memory-tracked instances

`getinstances` should be able to return [instances](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 outside of [`game`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/DataModel)
.

`getinstances` retrieves **every [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
** from the registry. Which means that instances that are/were parented to `nil` will also be returned.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-0-1) function getinstances(): { Instance }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Finding a nil-parented instance |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getinstances/#__codelineno-1-8) | `local dummy_part = Instance.new("Part") dummy_part.Parent = nil for _, instance in pairs(getinstances()) do     if instance == dummy_part then        print("Found the dummy part!")    end end` |

Back to top

# firetouchinterest - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#firetouchinterest)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/firetouchinterest.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/firetouchinterest.md "View source of this page")

`firetouchinterest`
===================

Avoid implementing in Luau

This function should **not be implemented** in Luau. Doing so exposes you to easy detection vectors.

`firetouchinterest` simulates a physical touch event between two [`BasePart`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BasePart)
 objects. It can emulate both the start and end of a [`Touched`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BasePart#Touched)
 event.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-0-1) function firetouchinterest(part1: BasePart, part2: BasePart, toggle: boolean | number): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `part1` | The initiating [`BasePart`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BasePart)<br>. |
| `part2` | The [`BasePart`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BasePart)<br> that should be touched. |
| `toggle` | Whether to simulate touch start or end. `true` or `0` simulates touch; `false` or `1` simulates un-touch. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Simulating a Touched event using 'true/false' |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-1-14) | `local dummy_part = Instance.new("Part") dummy_part.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -200, 0) dummy_part.Anchored = true dummy_part.Parent = workspace dummy_part.Touched:Connect(function(part)     print(part.Name .. " touched the dummy part!") end) local player_head = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head firetouchinterest(player_head, dummy_part, true) -- Simulate touch task.wait(0.5) firetouchinterest(player_head, dummy_part, false) -- Simulate un-touch` |

### Example 2

| Simulating a Touched event using '0/1' |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/firetouchinterest/#__codelineno-2-14) | `local dummy_part = Instance.new("Part") dummy_part.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -200, 0) dummy_part.Anchored = true dummy_part.Parent = workspace dummy_part.Touched:Connect(function(part)     print(part.Name .. " touched the dummy part!") end) local player_head = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head firetouchinterest(player_head, dummy_part, 0) -- Simulate touch task.wait(0.5) firetouchinterest(player_head, dummy_part, 1) -- Simulate un-touch` |

Back to top

# getnilinstances - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#getnilinstances)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Instances/getnilinstances.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Instances/getnilinstances.md "View source of this page")

`getnilinstances`
=================

`getnilinstances` returns a list of [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 objects that are **currently unparented**. These instances exist in memory but are no longer part of the [`DataModel`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/DataModel)
 hierarchy.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-0-1) function getnilinstances(): { Instance }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Detecting a detached part |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Instances/getnilinstances/#__codelineno-1-6) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") for _, instance in pairs(getnilinstances()) do     if instance == part then        print("Found our unattached part!")    end end` |

# Metatable - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/#metatable)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Metatable/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Metatable/README.md "View source of this page")

Metatable
=========

The **Metatable** library enables advanced interaction with [metatables](https://create.roblox.com/docs/luau/metatables)
 in Luau. It provides direct access to core metamethods and internal table behaviours - including those normally protected or hidden via `__metatable` locks.

This library is especially useful when trying to modify or access hidden things within locked Roblox objects.

* * *

What is a metatable?
--------------------

A [**metatable**](https://create.roblox.com/docs/luau/metatables)
 in Luau is a hidden table that can change the behavior of another table. Metatables allow you to define custom behaviors like operator overloading, default values, or interception of table reads and writes using special fields like [`__index`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/luau/metatables#metamethods)
 or [`__newindex`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/luau/metatables#metamethods)
.

In Roblox, this is useful for exposing metatables of Roblox Instances so that they can be leveraged for hooking or other modifications.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Metatable library, you can:

*   **Retrieve** hidden metatables using [`getrawmetatable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getrawmetatable/)
    
*   **Replace** a table or object's metatable with [`setrawmetatable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/)
    
*   **Control** whether a table is locked using [`setreadonly`](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setreadonly/)
    
*   **Check** whether a table is locked with [`isreadonly`](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/isreadonly/)
    

Back to top

---

# getnamecallmethod - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#getnamecallmethod)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Metatable/getnamecallmethod.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Metatable/getnamecallmethod.md "View source of this page")

`getnamecallmethod`
===================

This function must be called from within a `__namecall` metatable hook, otherwise it will return `nil`.

`getnamecallmethod` returns the name of the method that invoked the [`__namecall`](https://devforum.roblox.com/t/how-do-i-get-namecall-method/2848439/5)
 metamethod.

When used **inside** a [`hookmetamethod`](https://docs.sunc.su/Closures/hookmetamethod/)
 hook targeting `__namecall`, it will attempt to retrieve the method being called (e.g. `InvokeServer`).

When used **outside** of said hook, this function will safely return `nil`.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-0-1) function getnamecallmethod(): string?`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Disallowing the usage of game:service() |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/getnamecallmethod/#__codelineno-1-12) | `local refs = {} refs.__namecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", function(...)     local self = ...    local method = getnamecallmethod()     if self == game and method == "service" then        error("Using game:service() is not allowed.")    end     return refs.__namecall(...) end)` |

Back to top

---

# setrawmetatable - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#setrawmetatable)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Metatable/setrawmetatable.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Metatable/setrawmetatable.md "View source of this page")

`setrawmetatable`
=================

`setrawmetatable` forcibly sets the metatable of a value, bypassing the `__metatable` protection field.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-0-1) function setrawmetatable<T>(object: T & ({ any } | userdata), metatable: { any }): T`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object` | The value whose metatable will be overwritten. |
| `metatable` | The new metatable to assign. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Overriding the metatable of a string |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Metatable/setrawmetatable/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local dummy_string = "Example" local string_metatable = setrawmetatable(dummy_string, {     __index = getgenv() }) print(string_metatable)          -- Output: Example print(string_metatable.getgenv)        -- Output: function: 0x...` |

`getrawmetatable` returns the raw metatable of an object, even if that object has a `__metatable` field set.

`identifyexecutor`
==================

`identifyexecutor` returns the name and version of the currently running executor.

This function is quite self-explanatory, you use it for logging/debugging purposes, idk - its quite basic.

The function returns a tuple of:

1.  `string` - The name/identifier of the executor.
2.  `string` - The version string of the executor.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/identifyexecutor/#__codelineno-0-1) function identifyexecutor(): (string, string)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Getting the current executor and version |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/identifyexecutor/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/identifyexecutor/#__codelineno-1-2) | `local exec_name, exec_version = identifyexecutor() print(exec_name, exec_version) -- Output: "YourExploitName 0.0.1"` |

# Miscellaneous - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/#miscellaneous)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Miscellaneous/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Miscellaneous/README.md "View source of this page")

Miscellaneous
=============

The **Miscellaneous** library contains functions that do not belong to a specific category.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Miscellaneous library, you can:

*   **Identify** the current executor and version using [`identifyexecutor`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/identifyexecutor/)
    
*   **Send HTTP requests** and receive full responses with [`request`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/)
    

* * *

What does [`request`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/)
 support?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [`request`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/)
 function supports a variety of features:

*   Custom HTTP methods (`GET`, `POST`, `PATCH`, `PUT`, `DELETE`)
*   Request and response headers
*   Request body and cookies
*   Built-in executor identification headers, such as `PREFIX-User-Identifier` and `PREFIX-Fingerprint`

* * *

What can't you do?
------------------

*   [`request`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/)
     is **synchronous** and yields until the server responds - it's not suitable for parallel messaging.
*   Some executors may restrict access to external domains (such as the Roblox API for account safety purposes) or block specific methods for security reasons.
*   [`identifyexecutor`](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/identifyexecutor/)
     should never be relied on as a secure identifier - it's for informational purposes only.

Back to top

---

# Reflection - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/#reflection)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/README.md "View source of this page")

Reflection
==========

The **Reflection** library allows access to and manipulation of hidden or non-scriptable properties of [Instances](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 and internal execution context. It is primarily used to bypass standard Luau restrictions in controlled environments.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Reflection library, you can:

*   **Read** hidden instance properties using [`gethiddenproperty`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/)
    
*   **Write** to hidden instance properties with [`sethiddenproperty`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/)
    
*   **Toggle and check** scriptability of properties using [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
     and [`isscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/)
    .
*   **Elevate** thread permissions with [`setthreadidentity`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/)
    
*   **Query** the current thread's permission level with [`getthreadidentity`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/getthreadidentity/)
    

These identities are internally refered to as [security context levels](https://github.com/Pseudoreality/Roblox-Identities/)
, and determine the permissions granted to a thread.

* * *

What can't you do?
------------------

While powerful, the Reflection library carries **detection risks** in sensitive environments:

*   [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
     is detectable by games that check for unusual access.
*   Using these methods irresponsibly may break core game logic or introduce unintended side effects.

Back to top

---

# gethiddenproperty - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#gethiddenproperty)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/gethiddenproperty.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/gethiddenproperty.md "View source of this page")

`gethiddenproperty`
===================

Avoid relying on [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
 to implement this function!

Some executors implement this function using [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
, which is limited and/or detectable.

`gethiddenproperty` retrieves the value of a hidden or non-scriptable property (e.g. `BinaryString`, `SharedString`, `SystemAddress`) from a given [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
, even if it would normally throw an error when accessed directly.

This function also returns whether the accessed property was hidden.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-0-1) function gethiddenproperty(instance: Instance, property_name: string): (any, boolean)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `instance` | The [instance](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> containing the hidden property. |
| `property_name` | The name of the property to access. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Reading a hidden property |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") print(gethiddenproperty(part, "Name"))       -- Output: Part, false print(gethiddenproperty(part, "DataCost"))   -- Output: 20, false print(gethiddenproperty(part, "NetworkOwnerV3"))   -- Output: -1, true` |

Back to top

# sethiddenproperty - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#sethiddenproperty)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/sethiddenproperty.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/sethiddenproperty.md "View source of this page")

`sethiddenproperty`
===================

Avoid relying on [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
 to implement this function

Some executors implement this function using [`setscriptable`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/)
, which is limited and/or detectable.

`sethiddenproperty` assigns a value to a hidden or non-scriptable property of an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
, even if that property is normally read-only or inaccessible.

It returns `true` if the property is hidden and was successfully written to, or `false` if the property wasn't hidden but was still updated.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-0-1) function sethiddenproperty(instance: Instance, property_name: string, property_value: any): boolean`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `instance` | The [instance](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> that owns the target property. |
| `property_name` | The name of the property to update. |
| `property_value` | The new value to assign to the property. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Setting a hidden property value |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/sethiddenproperty/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") print(gethiddenproperty(part, "DataCost")) -- Output: 20, true sethiddenproperty(part, "DataCost", 100) print(gethiddenproperty(part, "DataCost")) -- Output: 100, true` |

Back to top

# setscriptable - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#setscriptable)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/setscriptable.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/setscriptable.md "View source of this page")

`setscriptable`
===============

Detection risks

`setscriptable` can expose detection vectors. Games may check whether certain properties are unexpectedly accessible, which can lead to detections.

Limited property support

Not all hidden properties can be obtained using this function.

`setscriptable` toggles the scriptability of a hidden or non-scriptable property on an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
. When a property is made scriptable, it can be accessed or assigned through standard indexing.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-0-1) function setscriptable(instance: Instance, property_name: string, state: boolean): boolean | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `instance` | The [Instance](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> that owns the target property. |
| `property_name` | The name of the property to make scriptable or un-scriptable. |
| `state` | Whether to enable (`true`) or disable (`false`) scriptability. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Temporarily enabling scriptability of a property |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setscriptable/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") setscriptable(part, "BottomParamA", true) print(part.BottomParamA) -- Output: -0.5 setscriptable(part, "BottomParamA", false) print(part.BottomParamA) -- Throws an error` |

Back to top

---

# isscriptable - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#isscriptable)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/isscriptable.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/isscriptable.md "View source of this page")

`isscriptable`
==============

`isscriptable` returns whether the given property of an [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)
 is scriptable (i.e. it does not have the `notscriptable` tag).

If it returns `true`, then the property is scriptable and can be indexed normally, and vice versa.

If it returns `nil`, then the property provided does not exist.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-0-1) function isscriptable(object: Instance, property: string): boolean | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `object` | The [`Instance`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Instance)<br> that owns the target property. |
| `property` | The name of the property to check. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Checking the scriptability of a property |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/isscriptable/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") setscriptable(part, "BottomParamA", false) print(isscriptable(part, "BottomParamA")) -- false` |

Back to top

---

# setthreadidentity - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#setthreadidentity)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Reflection/setthreadidentity.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Reflection/setthreadidentity.md "View source of this page")

`setthreadidentity`
===================

`setthreadidentity` sets the current [Luau thread](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/libraries/coroutine#running)
 identity and capabilities matching that identity.

This is commonly used alongside functions like [`gethiddenproperty`](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/gethiddenproperty/)
 or [`getconnections`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/)
 which may require elevated access.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-0-1) function setthreadidentity(id: number): ()`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `id` | The identity level to set the current thread to. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Changing thread identity for privileged access |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Reflection/setthreadidentity/#__codelineno-1-5) | `setthreadidentity(2) print(pcall(function() return game.CoreGui end)) -- Output: false (restricted access) setthreadidentity(8) print(pcall(function() return game.CoreGui end)) -- Output: true Instance` |

Back to top

# Scripts - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/#scripts)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/README.md "View source of this page")

Scripts
=======

The **Scripts** library provides advanced functions for inspecting and interacting with script objects. It allows you to analyse bytecode, retrieve closures and environments, and simulate the loading or running of scripts.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Scripts library, you can:

*   **Read compiled bytecode** from scripts using [`getscriptbytecode`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/)
    
*   **Get the bytecode hash** of a script using [`getscripthash`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/)
    
*   **Create a new closure based off of the script's bytecode** using [`getscriptclosure`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/)
    
*   **Access script environments** with [`getsenv`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/)
    
*   **Enumerate script instances** using [`getscripts`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/)
     and [`getrunningscripts`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/)
    
*   **List loaded modules** via [`getloadedmodules`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/)
    
*   **Determine the current script** executing via [`getcallingscript`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/)
    
*   **Compile and run code at runtime** using [`loadstring`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/)
    

Back to top

---

# getscriptbytecode - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#getscriptbytecode)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getscriptbytecode.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getscriptbytecode.md "View source of this page")

`getscriptbytecode`
===================

Notes on `getscriptbytecode`

This function should return `nil` if the script has no bytecode. This makes it easier to check for absence consistently across executors.

`getscriptbytecode` retrieves the bytecode of a [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
, and [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-0-1) function getscriptbytecode(script: BaseScript | ModuleScript): string | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `script` | The script instance to retrieve the bytecode from. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Reading the bytecode of a running script |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptbytecode/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local animate = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Animate") print(getscriptbytecode(animate)) -- Returns bytecode as a string print(getscriptbytecode(Instance.new("LocalScript"))) -- Output: nil` |

# getcallingscript - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#getcallingscript)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getcallingscript.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getcallingscript.md "View source of this page")

`getcallingscript`
==================

Notes on `getcallingscript`

If a game script is executing, and `getcallingscript` is called, it must return the proper [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, or [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 - even if the [`script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/RobloxGlobals#script)
 global for said script is set to `nil`.

`getcallingscript` returns the [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, or [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 that **triggered the current code execution**.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-0-1) function getcallingscript(): BaseScript | ModuleScript | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Detecting the calling script in a hook |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getcallingscript/#__codelineno-1-13) | `local old; old = hookmetamethod(game, "__index", function(self, key)     if not checkcaller() then        local caller = getcallingscript()        warn("__index access from script:", caller and caller:GetFullName() or "Unknown")         hookmetamethod(game, "__index", old) -- Restore the original        return old(self, key)    end     return old(self, key) end) print(getcallingscript()) -- Output: nil, since we called from an executor thread` |

# request - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#request)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Miscellaneous/request.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Miscellaneous/request.md "View source of this page")

`request`
=========

`request` sends a [HTTP request](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP)
 to the given URL using the provided configuration table. It yields until the request is complete and returns a structured response.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-1) type RequestOptions = {     [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-2)     Url: string,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-3)     Method: "GET" | "HEAD" | "POST" | "PUT" | "DELETE" | "OPTIONS" | "PATCH",    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-4)     Body: string?,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-5)     Headers: { [string]: string }?,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-6)     Cookies: { [string]: string }? [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-7) } [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-8)[](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-9) type Response = {     [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-10)     Success: boolean,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-11)     Body: string,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-12)     StatusCode: number,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-13)     StatusMessage: string,    [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-14)     Headers: { [string]: string } [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-15) } [](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-16)[](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-0-17) function request(options: RequestOptions): Response`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `options` | A table of fields defining the HTTP request. |

### `RequestOptions` Fields

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Url` | `string` | The target URL. |
| `Method` | `string` | The HTTP [method](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Reference/Methods)<br> (`GET`, `HEAD`, `POST`, `PUT`, `DELETE`, `OPTIONS` or `PATCH`). |
| `Body` | `string?` | (Optional) The request payload. |
| `Headers` | `{ [string]: string }?` | (Optional) Dictionary of HTTP [headers](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Reference/Headers)<br>. |
| `Cookies` | `{ [string]: string }?` | (Optional) Dictionary of [cookies](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Reference/Headers/Cookie)<br>. |

### `Response` Fields

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Success` | `boolean` | Whether the request was successful. |
| `Body` | `string` | The returned response body. |
| `StatusCode` | `number` | The numeric HTTP [status code](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Reference/Status)<br>. |
| `StatusMessage` | `string` | The human-readable status description. |
| `Headers` | `{ [string]: string }` | Dictionary of response [headers](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Reference/Headers)<br>. |

### Automatically added Headers

Executors will attach this unique header automatically:

| Header | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `PREFIX-User-Identifier` | Unique user ID that stays consistent across devices for the same user. |
| `PREFIX-Fingerprint` | Hardware-bound identifier (HWID) of the client's machine. |
| [`User-Agent`](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User-Agent_header) | Executor name and version string. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Basic GET request with fingerprint lookup |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-14)<br>[15](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-15)<br>[16](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-16)<br>[17](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-17)<br>[18](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-1-18) | `local response = request({     Url = "http://httpbin.org/get",    Method = "GET", }) local decoded = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response.Body) local retrieved_fingerprint for key in pairs(decoded.headers) do     if key:match("Fingerprint") then        retrieved_fingerprint = key        break    end end print(response.StatusCode)         -- Output: 200 print(response.Success)            -- Output: true print(retrieved_fingerprint)        -- Output: PREFIX-Fingerprint` |

### Example 2

| Basic POST request with payload |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-8)<br>[9](https://docs.sunc.su/Miscellaneous/request/#__codelineno-2-9) | `local response = request({     Url = "http://httpbin.org/post",    Method = "POST",    Body = "Example" }) print(response.StatusMessage)                               -- Output: OK print(response.StatusCode)                                  -- Output: 200 print(game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response.Body).data) -- Output: Example` |

Back to top

# getrunningscripts - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#getrunningscripts)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getrunningscripts.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getrunningscripts.md "View source of this page")

`getrunningscripts`
===================

Notes on `getrunningscripts`

This function should return all the scripts mentioned below, regardless of any mutations made to itself or its environment.

This also includes scripts whose [`script` global variable](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/RobloxGlobals#script)
 is set to `nil` or reassigned - i.e. `getrunningscripts` should still include said scripts.

`getrunningscripts` returns a list of **all running scripts** in the caller's global state. This includes [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, and [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 instances - excluding [`CoreScripts`](https://robloxapi.github.io/ref/class/CoreScript.html)
 by default.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-0-1) function getrunningscripts(): { BaseScript | ModuleScript }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Checking for active scripts in the session |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getrunningscripts/#__codelineno-1-11) | `local running = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Animate") local inactive = Instance.new("LocalScript") -- Not running because no bytecode to run for _, script in pairs(getrunningscripts()) do     if script == running then        print("Found the running Animate script.")    elseif script == inactive then        print("This should never print.")        print("If this did print, then you have just experienced 1 in a quintillion chance of BITS FLIPPING from radiation. Do you live inside a nuclear reactor?")    end end` |

# getscriptclosure - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#getscriptclosure)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getscriptclosure.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getscriptclosure.md "View source of this page")

`getscriptclosure`
==================

Closure is compiled from the script's bytecode, not an active one

The function returned by `getscriptclosure` is a **new closure** compiled from the script's bytecode. It is not the function used by the game script, but has identical metadata. This function is usually used to retrieve constants from a script.

Not all scripts have bytecode

If the script has no compiled bytecode, this function will return `nil`.

`getscriptclosure` creates and returns a Luau **function closure** from the compiled bytecode of a [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, or [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
.

This function is often used to **extract constants or behaviour** from scripts without needing to run them inside the game.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-0-1) function getscriptclosure(script: BaseScript | ModuleScript): (...any) -> (...any) | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `script` | The script instance to convert into a function. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Retrieving a script's closure |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscriptclosure/#__codelineno-1-7) | `local animate = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Animate") local closure = getscriptclosure(animate) print(typeof(closure)) -- Output: function 0x.... print(getscriptclosure(Instance.new("LocalScript"))) -- Output: nil` |

Back to top

# getscripthash - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#getscripthash)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getscripthash.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getscripthash.md "View source of this page")

`getscripthash`
===============

Do not decrypt or decompress the bytecode

The hash must be computed **on the encrypted, compressed bytecode** - not after any modification.  
This function should also return `nil` if the script has no bytecode.

`getscripthash` returns a [SHA-384 hash](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SHA-3)
 in **_hexadecimal format_** of the raw bytecode for a given [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, or [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
.

This is useful for **identifying scripts** by their content, especially when checking for known modules or verifying integrity.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-0-1) function getscripthash(script: BaseScript | ModuleScript): string | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `script` | The [BaseScript](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BaseScript)<br> or [ModuleScript](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)<br> instance to hash. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Hashing a live script |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripthash/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local Animate = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Animate") print(getscripthash(Animate)) -- Output: 384-bit hash string print(getscripthash(Instance.new("LocalScript"))) -- Output: nil` |

Back to top

---

# getloadedmodules - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#getloadedmodules)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getloadedmodules.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getloadedmodules.md "View source of this page")

`getloadedmodules`
==================

Returns only loaded modules

This function **only** returns [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 instances that have already been loaded using [`require`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#require)
.  
It does **not** return all [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 objects in the game - for that, use [`getscripts`](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/)
.

`getloadedmodules` returns a list of all [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 instances that have been **loaded** (e.g. [`require`'d](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#require)
).

This includes only modules with completed executions, and **excludes** any modules that errored or haven't been required yet.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-0-1) function getloadedmodules(): { ModuleScript }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Checking if a module has been loaded |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-11)<br>[12](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-12)<br>[13](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-13)<br>[14](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getloadedmodules/#__codelineno-1-14) | `local loaded = Instance.new("ModuleScript") local not_loaded = Instance.new("ModuleScript") pcall(require, loaded) for _, module in pairs(getloadedmodules()) do     if module == loaded then        -- The first modulescript was found because it was required in line 4        print("Found loaded module!")    elseif module == notLoaded then        -- The second modulescript should NOT be found because it was never required        print("This should never appear.")    end end` |

Back to top

# getsenv - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#getsenv)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getsenv.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getsenv.md "View source of this page")

`getsenv`
=========

Only works on active scripts

This function will throw an error if the script isn't currently running. If the script is running but on a different Lua State (such as on an [Actor](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Actor)
), the function will return nil instead.

`getsenv` returns the **global environment table** of a given [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, or [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
.

This environment contains **all global variables and functions** available to the target script, such as custom-defined functions or state values.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-0-1) function getsenv(script: BaseScript | ModuleScript): { [any]: any } | nil`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `script` | The script instance whose environment should be retrieved. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Accessing a script's internal environment |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getsenv/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local animate = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Animate") local env = getsenv(animate) print(typeof(env.onSwimming)) -- Output: function` |

Back to top

# getscripts - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#getscripts)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/getscripts.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/getscripts.md "View source of this page")

`getscripts`
============

`getscripts` returns a list of **all [`Script`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Script)
, [`LocalScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/LocalScript)
, and [`ModuleScript`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/ModuleScript)
 instances** present.

This function excludes [`CoreScripts`](https://robloxapi.github.io/ref/class/CoreScript.html)
 by default.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-0-1) function getscripts(): { BaseScript | ModuleScript }`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| _(none)_ | This function takes no parameters. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Locating a known script instance |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/getscripts/#__codelineno-1-8) | `local dummy_script = Instance.new("LocalScript") dummy_script.Name = "TestScript" for _, script in pairs(getscripts()) do     if script == dummy_script then        print("Found the dummy script!")    end end` |

Back to top

# Signals - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/#signals)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Signals/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Signals/README.md "View source of this page")

Signals
=======

The **Signals** library provides functions for inspecting and manipulating [`RBXScriptSignal`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptSignal)
 and [`RBXScriptConnection`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptConnection)
 objects.

* * *

What is a signal?
-----------------

A [signal](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptSignal)
 in Roblox is an event emitter - an object that can have functions connected to it, which are triggered when something happens. For example, [`Part.Touched`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/BasePart#Touched)
 is a signal that fires when something touches a part.

Signals are backed by objects called **connections**, which are instances of an [`RBXScriptConnection`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptConnection)
.

Exploits will return their own [custom connection object](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/Connection/)
 when using `getconnections`.

* * *

What can you do?
----------------

With the Signals library, you can:

*   **Get all connections** attached to a signal using [`getconnections`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/)
    .
*   **Fire** a signal's Luau connections using [`firesignal`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/)
    .
*   **Replicate signals to the server** with [`replicatesignal`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/)
    , if supported by the signal.

For a list of known replicable signals, click [this](https://rubis.app/markdown-focus/?scrap=AIOzG1Di7NSLADKE&accent=a460f9)
.

Back to top

---

# loadstring - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#loadstring)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Scripts/loadstring.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Scripts/loadstring.md "View source of this page")

`loadstring`
============

Unsafe by design

Compiles the given string, and returns it runnable in a function. The environment must become unsafe after this function is called due to it allowing the modification of globals uncontrollably (see [`setfenv`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#setfenv)
/[`getfenv`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/globals/LuaGlobals#getfenv)
 documentation).

Should error when compilation fails

This function should return `nil` and an error message if the provided code fails to compile.

`loadstring` compiles a string of Luau code and returns it as a runnable function. If the code has errors, `nil` is returned and an error message is output.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-0-1) function loadstring<A...>(source: string, chunkname: string?): (((A...) -> any) | nil, string?)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `source` | The source code string to compile. |
| `chunkname?` | Custom chunk name. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Compiling and running source code successfully |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-1-5) | `loadstring([[     placeholder = {"Example"} ]])() print(placeholder[1]) -- Output: Example` |

* * *

### Example 2

| Using a custom chunk name while also getting an error |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Scripts/loadstring/#__codelineno-2-4) | `local func, err = loadstring("Example = ", "CustomChunk") print(func) -- Output: nil print(err)  -- Output: [string "CustomChunk"]:1: Expected identifier when parsing expression, got <eof>` |

Back to top

# firesignal - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#firesignal)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Signals/firesignal.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Signals/firesignal.md "View source of this page")

`firesignal`
============

Firing mode

This function will invoke all the connections of the signal **immediately**, ignoring the [`Workspace.SignalBehaviour`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/classes/Workspace#SignalBehavior)
 property.

`firesignal` Invokes all Luau [connections](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptConnection)
 connected to a given [`RBXScriptSignal`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptSignal)
.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-0-1) function firesignal(signal: RBXScriptSignal, ...: any?)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `signal` | The signal whose connections you want to manually fire. |
| `...?` | The arguments to pass to the connected functions. |

* * *

Example
-------

| Manually firing a signal with and without arguments |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/firesignal/#__codelineno-1-8) | `local part = Instance.new("Part") part.ChildAdded:Connect(function(arg1)     print(typeof(arg1)) end) firesignal(part.ChildAdded)            -- Output: nil firesignal(part.ChildAdded, workspace) -- Output: Instance` |

# The Connection object - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/Connection/#the-connection-object)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Signals/Connection.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Signals/Connection.md "View source of this page")

The `Connection` object
=======================

Notes on the `Connection` object

The retrieved connection object will only have the listed methods and fields, since it's a custom object

A `Connection` object represents an active link to a signal's callback. These are returned by [`getconnections`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/)
 and allow inspection and manipulation over connections/signals.

* * *

Fields
------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Enabled` | `boolean` | Whether the connection is currently active and will respond to events. |
| `ForeignState` | `boolean` | `true` if the connection was made from a foreign Luau state (e.g. CoreScript). |
| `LuaConnection` | `boolean` | `true` if the connection was created from Luau, not C. |
| `Function` | `(...any) -> (...any)?` | The bound function, or `nil` if foreign or non-Luau contexts. |
| `Thread` | `thread?` | The thread that created the connection, or `nil` in foreign or non-Luau contexts. |

Foreign and C-state behavior

If the connection originates from a foreign Lua state or is a C-level connection, `Function` and `Thread` will be `nil` and their `ForeignState` property will be `true`. This is due to neither `Function` or `Thread` existing on the current Luau VM.

* * *

Methods
-------

| Method Signature | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Connection:Fire(...: any): ()` | Fires the connected function with given arguments. |
| `Connection:Defer(...: any): ()` | Defers execution using [`task.defer`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/libraries/task#defer)<br>. |
| `Connection:Disconnect(): ()` | Disconnects the connection from the signal. |
| `Connection:Disable(): ()` | Prevents the connection from receiving events. |
| `Connection:Enable(): ()` | Re-enables a previously disabled connection. |

Back to top

---

# getconnections - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#getconnections)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Signals/getconnections.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Signals/getconnections.md "View source of this page")

`getconnections`
================

A `Connection`, in the context of `RBXScriptSignal`, refers to **a subscription between the signal (event) and the function to execute when it fires** - not the social 'connections' of a user.

Your game may crash if C connections are not properly supported.

`getconnections` retrieves a list of [`Connection`](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/Connection/)
 objects currently attached to a given [`RBXScriptSignal`](https://create.roblox.com/docs/reference/engine/datatypes/RBXScriptSignal)
.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-0-1) function getconnections(signal: RBXScriptSignal): {Connection}`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `signal` | The signal to inspect for active connections. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Inspecting and invoking a Luau connection |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-5)<br>[6](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-6)<br>[7](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-7)<br>[8](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-8)<br>[9](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-1-9) | `local folder = Instance.new("Folder") folder.ChildAdded:Connect(function()     return "Triggered" end) local connection = getconnections(folder.ChildAdded)[1] -- First connection in the list print(connection.Function())     -- Output: Triggered print(connection:Fire()) -- Same as above, Output: Triggered print(typeof(connection.Thread)) -- Output: thread` |

### Example 2

| Accessing a foreign/C connection |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/getconnections/#__codelineno-2-3) | `local cconnection = getconnections(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Idled)[1] print(cconnection.Function)  -- Output: nil print(cconnection.Thread)    -- Output: nil` |

Back to top

# replicatesignal - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#replicatesignal)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/Signals/replicatesignal.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/Signals/replicatesignal.md "View source of this page")

`replicatesignal`
=================

Signal arguments must match

Some signals require specific argument structures. If incorrect arguments are passed, an error must be thrown.

Notes on `replicatesignal`

For an accurate result from the examples, test the function in [our game](https://www.roblox.com/games/133609342474444/ROBLOCKS-STOP-PMOING-ME)
.

`replicatesignal` replicates a signal to the server with the provided arguments, if possible. The arguments must also match accordingly to the signal itself. To know a signal's arguments, visit [this](https://robloxapi.github.io/ref/)
.

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-0-1) function replicatesignal(signal: RBXScriptSignal, ...: any?)`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `signal` | The signal to replicate to the server. |
| `...?` | Arguments to pass to the signal. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Example 1

| Replicating a ClickDetector interaction |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local detector = workspace.replicatesigmal.ClickDetector replicatesignal(detector.MouseActionReplicated, game.Players.LocalPlayer, 0) task.wait(0.1) print(game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("MouseClickReplicated")) -- Output: true` |

### Example 2

| Incorrect argument usage |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-1)<br> [2](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-2)<br> [3](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-3)<br> [4](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-4)<br> [5](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-5)<br> [6](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-6)<br> [7](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-7)<br> [8](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-8)<br> [9](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-9)<br>[10](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-10)<br>[11](https://docs.sunc.su/Signals/replicatesignal/#__codelineno-2-11) | `local ui_frame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ScreenGui.Frame -- These will throw an error. replicatesignal(ui_frame.MouseWheelForward) replicatesignal(ui_frame.MouseWheelForward, 121) -- This succeeds replicatesignal(ui_frame.MouseWheelForward, 121, 214) task.wait(0.1) print(game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetAttribute("MouseWheelForwardReplicated")) -- Output: true` |

# WebSocket class - sUNC Documentation

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#websocket-class)

[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/edit/main/docs/WebSocket/README.md "Edit this page")
[](https://github.com/sUNC-Utilities/docs.sunc.su/raw/main/docs/WebSocket/README.md "View source of this page")

WebSocket class
===============

This is a WebSocket client only, meaning you won't be able to create a server with this library.

The sUNC test explicitly checks for `wss` (secure) support.

The `WebSocket` class provides a lightweight interface for establishing and working with WebSocket connections. It allows scripts to **send** and **receive** messages over a persistent connection to a [WebSocket](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WebSocket)
 server.

* * *

Constructor
-----------

Attempts to create a new connection to the provided URL. The URL must be a valid WebSocket server URL, typically starting with `ws://` (unsecure) or `wss://` (secure).

`[](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-0-1) function WebSocket.connect(url: string): WebSocket`

Parameters
----------

| Parameter | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `url` | A WebSocket URL. |

* * *

Events
------

Signals that allow you handle events that occur during the WebSocket's lifetime, such as opening, receiving messages, or closing.

| Event | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `OnMessage(message: string): ()` | Triggered when a message is received over the WebSocket connection. |
| `OnClose(): ()` | Triggered when the WebSocket connection closes. |

Methods
-------

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `Send(message: string): ()` | Sends a message over the WebSocket connection. |
| `Close(): ()` | Closes the WebSocket connection. |

* * *

Examples
--------

### Using the `OnMessage` event, and `Send` method

| Responding to incoming messages |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-1-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-1-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-1-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-1-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-1-5) | `local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.events") ws.OnMessage:Connect(function(message)     print(message) end) ws:Send("Hello") -- Output: Hello` |

* * *

### Using the `OnClose` event, and `Close` method

| Receive a closing message and catch it via OnClose |     |
| --- | --- |
| [1](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-2-1)<br>[2](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-2-2)<br>[3](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-2-3)<br>[4](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-2-4)<br>[5](https://docs.sunc.su/WebSocket/#__codelineno-2-5) | `local ws = WebSocket.connect("wss://echo.websocket.events") ws.OnClose:Connect(function()     print("Closed") end) ws:Close() -- Output: Closed` |

Back to top
